      <p><b>Eritrea</b> is a country on the <a href="/wiki/East_Africa" title="East Africa">eastern</a> coast of <a href="/wiki/Africa" title="Africa">Africa</a>. Its official name is <b>The State of Eritrea</b>. </p>

                    <p>Apostolic Succession and Missionary Origins: </p> 
                    <ul>
                     <li><a href="/w/index.php?title=Frumentius&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Frumentius (not yet started)">Frumentius</a> (328 AD <a href="/wiki/Axum" title="Axum">Axum</a>)<sup id="cite_ref-isbn0-313-32273-2_25-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-isbn0-313-32273-2-25">[25]</a></sup></li>

      <h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Geography">Geography</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Eritrea&amp;veaction=edit&amp;section=1" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Change section: Geography">change</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Eritrea&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Change section: Geography">change source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2> 
      <div class="thumb tleft">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
        <a href="/wiki/File:Eritrean_Highlands.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a4/Eritrean_Highlands.jpg/220px-Eritrean_Highlands.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="165" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a4/Eritrean_Highlands.jpg/330px-Eritrean_Highlands.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a4/Eritrean_Highlands.jpg/440px-Eritrean_Highlands.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1600" data-file-height="1200"></a> 
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a href="/wiki/File:Eritrean_Highlands.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a>
         </div>Eritrean highlands.
        </div>
       </div>
      </div> 
      <p>Eritrea is located on the <a href="/wiki/Coast" title="Coast">coast</a> on the <a href="/wiki/Red_Sea" title="Red Sea">Red Sea</a>. It is north of the <a href="/wiki/Bab-el-Mandeb" title="Bab-el-Mandeb">Bab-el-Mandeb</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Horn_of_Africa" title="Horn of Africa">Horn of Africa</a>. Eritrea has borders with the countries of <a href="/wiki/Sudan" title="Sudan">Sudan</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ethiopia" title="Ethiopia">Ethiopia</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Djibouti" title="Djibouti">Djibouti</a>. The land <a href="/wiki/Area" title="Area">area</a> of Eritrea is 101,000&nbsp;km², and it is one of the smallest countries in Africa.<sup id="cite_ref-Factbook_39-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Factbook-39">[39]</a></sup> </p> 
      <h2><span class="mw-headline" id="History">History</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Eritrea&amp;veaction=edit&amp;section=2" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Change section: History">change</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Eritrea&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Change section: History">change source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2> 
      <p>Eritrea became an <a href="/wiki/Independence" title="Independence">independent</a> country on <a href="/wiki/24_May" class="mw-redirect" title="24 May">24 May</a> <a href="/wiki/1993" title="1993">1993</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Factbook_39-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Factbook-39">[39]</a></sup> It is one of the newest countries in the world. </p>
      <p>Many different countries have ruled the land that is now called Eritrea. Between <a href="/wiki/1885" title="1885">1885</a> and <a href="/wiki/1941" title="1941">1941</a> it was a <a href="/wiki/Colony" title="Colony">colony</a> of <a href="/wiki/Italy" title="Italy">Italy</a>. Between <a href="/wiki/1941" title="1941">1941</a> and <a href="/wiki/1952" title="1952">1952</a>, the <a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">United Nations</a> put it under the protection of <a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom" title="United Kingdom">United Kingdom</a>. After 1952, Eritrea became a part of <a href="/wiki/Ethiopia" title="Ethiopia">Ethiopia</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Factbook_39-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Factbook-39">[39]</a></sup> This was the reason for a long <a href="/wiki/War" title="War">civil war</a> between the Eritreans and the government of Ethiopia. </p>
      <p>Eventually, in 1993, Eritrea became an independent country after a <a href="/wiki/Vote" class="mw-redirect" title="Vote">vote</a> by its people.<sup id="cite_ref-Factbook_39-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Factbook-39">[39]</a></sup> </p> 
      <h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Government">Government</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Eritrea&amp;veaction=edit&amp;section=3" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Change section: Government">change</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Eritrea&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Change section: Government">change source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2> 
      <p>Eritrea is known for being the most oppressive country in Africa, sometimes considered to be the "North Korea of Africa".<sup id="cite_ref-40" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-40">[40]</a></sup> The nation has been accused of many human rights violations, severely limited freedoms, and many arbitrary (made-up) arrests. </p> 
      <h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Administrative_divisions">Administrative divisions</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Eritrea&amp;veaction=edit&amp;section=4" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Change section: Administrative divisions">change</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Eritrea&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Change section: Administrative divisions">change source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2> 
      <p>Eritrea is divided into six administrative regions. These areas are then divided into 58 districts. </p> 
      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:292px;">
        <a href="/wiki/File:Eritrea,_administrative_divisions_-_Nmbrs_-_colored.svg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b6/Eritrea%2C_administrative_divisions_-_Nmbrs_-_colored.svg/290px-Eritrea%2C_administrative_divisions_-_Nmbrs_-_colored.svg.png" decoding="async" width="290" height="238" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b6/Eritrea%2C_administrative_divisions_-_Nmbrs_-_colored.svg/435px-Eritrea%2C_administrative_divisions_-_Nmbrs_-_colored.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b6/Eritrea%2C_administrative_divisions_-_Nmbrs_-_colored.svg/580px-Eritrea%2C_administrative_divisions_-_Nmbrs_-_colored.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1844" data-file-height="1514"></a> 
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a href="/wiki/File:Eritrea,_administrative_divisions_-_Nmbrs_-_colored.svg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a>
         </div>A map of Eritrea regions. 1.Northern Red Sea, 2.Anseba, 3.Gash-Barka, 4.Central(to right), 5.Southern, 6.Southern Red Sea
        </div>

      </div>

      <h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Culture">Culture</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Eritrea&amp;veaction=edit&amp;section=5" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Change section: Culture">change</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Eritrea&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Change section: Culture">change source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2> 
      <p>The <a href="/wiki/Population" title="Population">population</a> of Eritrea is about 5.6&nbsp;million.<sup id="cite_ref-Factbook_39-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Factbook-39">[39]</a></sup> About 0.5&nbsp;million people live in Asmara. People from Eritrea are called <b>Eritreans</b>. Most of them speak <i>Tigrinya</i> or <i>Tigre</i> as their first <a href="/wiki/Language" title="***REMOVED***">language</a>. The people usually use Tigrinya or <a href="/wiki/Arabic_language" title="Arabic language">Arabic</a> for official business. </p>
      <p>Eritrea has nine ethnic groups. These are the Afar people, the Bilen people, the Hedareb people, the Kunama, the Nara, the Rashaida, the Saho, the Tigre, and Tigray-Tigrinya. </p>
      <p>The <a href="/wiki/Currency" title="Currency">currency</a> of Eritrea is called the <b>Nakfa</b>. Eritrea is a very poor country. Almost half of Eritrea's <a href="/wiki/Economy" title="Economy">economy</a> comes from Eritreans who live abroad. They send money home to their families. Most of the rest comes from <a href="/wiki/Farming" title="Farming">farming</a>. </p>
      <p><a href="/wiki/Association_football" title="Association football">Football</a> and <a href="/wiki/Cycling" class="mw-redirect" title="Cycling">cycling</a> are the most popular sports in Eritrea. In recent years, Eritrean athletes have also seen increasing success in the international arena. </p>
